***lende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lende</a> (91279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lenden.html>lenden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lendin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*landinō</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*landīnō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lenden.html>lenden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lendenen.html>lendenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>loin, bottom part of the back</li>
<li>flank, side</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lende</a></i>, shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*gelende</i>, an unattested variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelande.html>gelande</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lenden.html>lenden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lendenen.html>lendenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>lendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fellow countryman</li>
<li>(close) neighbour</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aangelande</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebuur.html>gebuur</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buur.html>buur</a></span></li></ul>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lendes.html>lendes</a> (127912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lendenu</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loins</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in compound <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lenden-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lende-</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*landį̄</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*landijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lendʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kidney, waist, loin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lendenen.html>lendenen</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loins</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lende.html>Lende</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">haunch, loin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">länd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">haunch, loin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">lend</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">loin</span>.

***lengen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lengen.html>lengen</a> (81867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lengen.html>lengen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lengen.html>lengen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*langijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lengen.html>lengen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become longer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lengen.html>lengen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nachten.html>nachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strengen.html>strengen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When the days <b>become longer</b>, the <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>nights</a> become colder.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lepeltje-lepeltje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lepeltje-lepeltje.html>lepeltje-lepeltje</a> (91274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Literally, “little spoon-little spoon”, referring to the resemblance of the spooning cuddling position to stacked <a href = vnd.unilang:spoons.html>spoons</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lepeltje-lepeltje.html>lepeltje-lepeltje</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>in the spooning position
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lepeltje-lepeltje.html>lepeltje-lepeltje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lange.html>lange</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> like <b>spooning</b> after a long evening.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***leper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leper.html>leper</a> (74712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lepre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">leprosy</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">leprae</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:lepra.html>lepra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λέπρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lépra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> leprosy.</li>
<li>A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> shunned; a pariah.</li></ol>

***leraar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leraar.html>leraar</a> (2042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leeraer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leerre</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to teach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leraar.html>leraar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leraren.html>leraren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leraartje.html>leraartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lerares.html>lerares</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A teacher, a person who gives lessons.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:docent.html>docent</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leerkracht.html>leerkracht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderwijzer.html>onderwijzer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Protestantism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A Protestant clergyman, a reverend.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dominee.html>dominee</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:predikant.html>predikant</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***leren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a> (453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lēren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to learn</li>

<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lederen.html>lederen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lederijn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lederen.html>lederen</a></i> (but also already <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></i>). ***lessen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lessen.html>lessen</a> (3356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lesschen</i>, from a merger of two <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*leskan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leskaną</i>; class 5 strong, intransitive.</li>
<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lesken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laskijaną</i>; class 1 weak, causative of the first verb.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lessen.html>lessen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quench (thirst)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take a lesson (usually a driving lesson)</li></ol>

***letten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:letten.html>letten</a> (2533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:letten.html>letten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:letten.html>letten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*latjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:letten.html>letten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay attention, to mind [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = to]</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prevent from doing something, to keep, to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></li>

***leu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leu.html>leu</a> (91267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably a <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> learned borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">leō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (around the 17th century), itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λέων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léōn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. If inherited from the nominative form, the expected result in Romanian would have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">*ieu</i> (as <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">iepure</i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">leporem</i>)<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>; furthermore, all the other Romance cognates <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> derived from the accusative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">leōnem</i> or genitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">leōnis</i> (and some <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> borrowings themselves). Cf. also <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">lăun</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">Lăune(le)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a river in Romania</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as well as <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">leoaie</i>.
</p><p>For the name of the currency, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> probably based on the Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">leeuwendaalder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lion thaler/<a href = vnd.unilang:dollar.html>dollar</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which depicted a lion; cf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">daalder</i>, also German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">löwenthaler</i>. This traces back to the 17th century, when the Dutch currency <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> used in the Romanian principalities. Another explanation gives the origin of this sense as a calque of Turkish <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">arslan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also used to refer to a type of currency with a lion on it<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>; see also <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">piastru</i> (English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">piastre</i>). Compare also the sense of currency with Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">лев</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:lev.html>lev</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_10">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ro"><a href = vnd.unilang:leu.html>leu</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-ro p-form-of" lang="ro"><a href = vnd.unilang:lei.html>lei</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lion</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leu.html>leu</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the Romanian unit of currency</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:leu.html>leu</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:financieel.html>financieel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:benaming.html>benaming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:munteenheden.html>munteenheden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Roemenië <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Moldavië

***leugendetector.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leugendetector.html>leugendetector</a> (14223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leugen.html>leugen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">detector</i>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie detector</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leugendetector.html>leugendetector</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leugendetectors.html>leugendetectors</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lie detector</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">contraption supposed to detect whether <a href = vnd.unilang:subjects.html>subjects</a> are lying or not</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In heraldry, the term "<a href = vnd.unilang:leuze.html>leuze</a>" denotes a <a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a> which goes above a shield, or on the border of the baldachin, whereas "<a href = vnd.unilang:wapenspreuk.html>wapenspreuk</a>" goes under the shield, on a scroll.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">watchword</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wapenspreuk.html>wapenspreuk</a></span></li></ul>

***leven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> (129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*libben</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*livon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*libjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to live</li></ol>
